\DoxyCodeLine{1295   \textcolor{comment}{// Torque allows and handles two types of expressions in the if protocol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1296   \textcolor{comment}{// automagically, ones that return TNode<BoolT> and those that use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1297   \textcolor{comment}{// BranchIf(..., Label* true, Label* false) idiom. Because the machinery to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1298   \textcolor{comment}{// handle this is embedded in the expression handling and to it's not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1299   \textcolor{comment}{// possible to make the decision to use CSA\_DCHECK or CSA\_DCHECK\_BRANCH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1300   \textcolor{comment}{// isn't trivial up-\/front. Secondly, on failure, the assert text should be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1301   \textcolor{comment}{// the corresponding Torque code, not the -\/gen.cc code, which would be the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1302   \textcolor{comment}{// case when using CSA\_DCHECK\_XXX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1303   Block* true\_block = \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1torque_1_1ImplementationVisitor_a1359f578571f344197cb4f9f8e1c79f7}{assembler}}().\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1torque_1_1CfgAssembler_a21c3a18fe21f64ec9a5f044e8e7a2ed0}{NewBlock}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1torque_1_1ImplementationVisitor_a1359f578571f344197cb4f9f8e1c79f7}{assembler}}().CurrentStack());}
